* - Speech recognition (listening)\n * - Text-to-speech (speaking)\n * - Form field extraction\n * - Command processing\n * - Backend integration\n */\n\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface AgenticConfig {\n  context?: string;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n  onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\n  onCommand?: (command: string,   \n    if (!globalRecognition) {\n      const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n      if (SR) {\n        globalRecognition = new SR();\n        globalRecognition.continuous = true;\n        globalRecognition.interimResults = true;\n        globalRecognition.lang = 'en-US';\n      }\n    }\n    \n    if (autoStart) {\n      setTimeout(() => 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') return;\n      console.error('[useAgentic] Recognition error:', event.error);\n      updateState('error');\n    };\n\n    const handleEnd = () => {\n      if  // Already started\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  const start = useCallback(() => {\n    globalSynth?.cancel();\n    isSpeakingRef.current = false;\n    shouldRunRef.current = true;\n } catch {}\n    globalSynth?.cancel();\n    updateState('idle');\n  }, [updateState]);\n\n  const toggle = useCallback(() => {\n    if (shouldRunRef.current) stop();\n    else start();\n  }, [start, \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udeb6 Creating WalkingCursor.tsx...\"\n\ncat > \"$CORE_DIR/WalkingCursor.tsx\" << 'WALKINGCURSOR'\n/**\n * WalkingCursor - THE ONE WALKER FOR ENTIRE APP\n * \n * Features:\n * - Auto-discovers interactive elements on page\n * - Walks between fields with smooth animation\n * - Works in modals, pages, anywhere\n * - Customizable appearance and behavior\n */\n\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface WalkingCursorProps {\n  enabled?: boolean;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n  walkSpeed?: number;        // ms between steps\n  pauseAtElement?: number;   // ms to pause at each element\n  selectors?: string;        // CSS selectors to target\n  excludeSelectors?: string; // CSS selectors to exclude\n  containerRef?: selectors = DEFAULT_SELECTORS,\n  excludeSelectors = DEFAULT_EXCLUDE,\n  containerRef,\n  onVisit,\n  onComplete,\n  variant = 'pointer',\n  color = '#06b6d4',\n  size = 24,\n  zIndex = 99999\n}) => {\n  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x: -100, y: -100 });\n  const [isWalking, setIsWalking] = useState(false);\n  const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0);\n  const [elements, setElements] = useState<HTMLElement[]>([]);\n  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);\n  \n  const walkingRef = useRef(false);\n  const timeoutRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);\n\n  // Discover elements\n  const discoverElements = useCallback(() => {\n    const container = containerRef?.current || document.body;\n    const found = container.querySelectorAll(selectors);\n    \n    const filtered = Array.from(found).filter(el => {\n      if (!el.matches || el.matches(excludeSelectors)) return false;\n      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\n      return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0;\n    }) as HTMLElement[];\n    \n    // Sort by position (top-to-bottom, left-to-right)\n    filtered.sort((a, b) => {\n      const aRect = a.getBoundingClientRect();\n      const bRect = b.getBoundingClientRect();\n      if (Math.abs(aRect.top - bRect.top) < 20) {\n        return aRect.left - bRect.left;\n      }\n      return aRect.top - bRect.top;\n    });\n    \n    setElements(filtered);\n    return filtered;\n  }, [selectors, excludeSelectors, containerRef]);\n\n  // Move to element\n  const moveToElement = window.pageYOffset;\n    \n    setPosition({\n      x: rect.left + scrollX + rect.width / 2,\n      y: rect.top + scrollY + rect.height / 2\n    });\n    \n    // Add highlight to element\n = useCallback(() => {\n    if (!walkingRef.current || elements.length === 0) return;\n    \n    const nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % elements.length;\n    const element = elements[nextIndex];\n    \n    if (element) {\n      moveToElement(element);\n      setCurrentIndex(nextIndex);\n      onVisit?.(element, nextIndex);\n      \n      if (nextIndex === 0 && currentIndex !== 0) {\n setIsVisible(true);\n    setCurrentIndex(0);\n    \n    // Move to first element\n    moveToElement(found[0]);\n    onVisit?.(found[0], 0);\n    \n    timeoutRef.current = setTimeout(walkNext, setIsWalking(false);\n    setIsVisible(false);\n    if (timeoutRef.current) {\n      clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current);\n      timeoutRef.current = null;\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Toggle walking\n  const toggleWalking = useCallback(() => {\n    if (isWalking) stopWalking();\n    else startWalking();\n  }, [isWalking, startWalking, stopWalking]);\n\n  // Auto-start\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (enabled && autoStart) {\n      const timer = setTimeout(startWalking, 1000);\n      return () => clearTimeout(timer);\n    }\n  }, [enabled, autoStart]);\n\n  // Cleanup\n  useEffect(() => {\n    return () => {\n      if (timeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current);\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  // Re-discover on resize\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const handleResize = () => discoverElements();\n    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);\n    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);\n  }, [discoverElements]);\n\n  if (!enabled || !isVisible) return null;\n\n  // Cursor variants\n  const cursorStyles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {\n    pointer: {\n      width: 0, height: 0,\n      borderLeft: `${size/2}px solid transparent`,\n      borderRight: `${size/2}px solid transparent`,\n      borderBottom: `${size}px solid ${color}`,\n      transform: 'rotate(-45deg)'\n    },\n    dot: {\n      width: size, height: size,\n      borderRadius: '50%',\n      background: color,\n      boxShadow: `0 0 ${size}px ${color}`\n    },\n    glow: {\n      width: size * 2, height: size * 2,\n      borderRadius: '50%',\n      background: `radial-gradient(circle, ${color} 0%, transparent 70%)`,\n      opacity: 0.8\n    },\n    hand: {\n      fontSize: size,\n      lineHeight: 1\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <div\n        style={{\n          position: 'absolute',\n          left: position.x,\n          top: position.y,\n          transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',\n          pointerEvents: 'none',\n          zIndex,\n          transition: `all ${walkSpeed * 0.3}ms ease-out`,\n          ...cursorStyles[variant]\n        }}\n      >\n        {variant === 'hand' && '\ud83d\udc46'}\n      </div>\n      \n      {/* Control button */}\n      <button\n        onClick={toggleWalking}\n        style={{\n          position: 'fixed',\n          bottom: 100,\n          right: 20,\n          width: 50,\n          height: 50,\n          borderRadius: '50%',\n          background: isWalking ? '#ef4444' : color,\n          border: 'none',\n          color: 'white',\n          fontSize: 20,\n          cursor: 'pointer',\n          zIndex: zIndex + 1,\n          boxShadow: '0 4px 15px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)'\n        }}\n        title={isWalking ? 'Stop Walker' : 'Start Walker'}\n      >\n        {isWalking ? '\u23f9' : '\ud83d\udeb6'}\n      </button>\n      \n      <style>{`\n        .walker-highlight {\n          outline: 3px solid ${color} !important;\n          outline-offset: 3px !important;\n          box-shadow: 0 0 20px ${color}40 !important;\n          transition: all 0.3s ease !important;\n        }\n      `}</style>\n    </>\n  );\n};\n\nexport default WalkingCursor;\nWALKINGCURSOR\n\necho \"  \u2705 WalkingCursor.tsx\"\n\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# 4. Filling\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\necho \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udcdd Creating VoiceFormFiller.tsx...\"\n\ncat > \"$CORE_DIR/VoiceFormFiller.tsx\" << 'VOICEFORMFILLER'\n/**\n * VoiceFormFiller - Universal form filling from voice\n * \n * Logic-only component that fills forms based on voice input\n */\n\nimport React, { useCallback } from 'react';\nimport { useAgentic } from './useAgentic';\n\ninterface FieldConfig {\n  selector: string;\n  voiceKeys?: string[];  // Multiple voice keys can map to same field\n  setter?: (value: string) => void;\n  transform?: (value: string) => string;  // Transform before setting\n}\n\ninterface VoiceFormFillerProps {\n  fields: Record<string, FieldConfig>;\n  context?: string;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n  onFill?: (field: string, value: string) => void;\n  onComplete?: (filledFields: string[]) => void;\n}\n\nexport const VoiceFormFiller: React.FC<VoiceFormFillerProps> = ({\n  fields,\n  context = 'form',\n  autoStart = false,\n  onFill,\n  onComplete\n}) => {\n  const filledFieldsRef = React.useRef<string[]>([]);\n\n  const handleFormData = useCallback(async (formData: Record<string, string>) => {\n    const agentic = useAgentic({ context });\n    \n    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(formData)) {\n      if (!value) continue;\n      \n      // Find matching field config\n      let fieldName: string | null = null;\n      let fieldConfig: FieldConfig | null = null;\n      \n      for (const [name, config] of Object.entries(fields)) {\n        const keys = config.voiceKeys || [name];\n        if (keys.some(k => k.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase())) {\n          fieldName = name;\n          fieldConfig = config;\n          break;\n        }\n      }\n      \n      if (!fieldName || !fieldConfig) continue;\n      \n      const transformedValue = fieldConfig.transform ? fieldConfig.transform(value) : value;\n      \n      await agentic.fillField(fieldConfig.selector, transformedValue, true);\n      fieldConfig.setter?.(transformedValue);\n      onFill?.(fieldName, transformedValue);\n      \n      if (!filledFieldsRef.current.includes(fieldName)) {\n        filledFieldsRef.current.push(fieldName);\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Check if all fields filled\n    if (filledFieldsRef.current.length === Object.keys(fields).length) {\n      onComplete?.(filledFieldsRef.current);\n    }\n  }, [fields, onFill, onComplete, context]);\n\n  useAgentic({\n    context,\n    autoStart,\n    onFormData: handleFormData\n  });\n\n  return null; // Logic-only component\n};\n\nexport default VoiceFormFiller;\nVOICEFORMFILLER\n\necho \"  \u2705 VoiceFormFiller.tsx\"\n\n#\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n# 6. \\\"$CORE_DIR\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# 1. useAgentic.ts - Core Hook\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udce6 Creating useAgentic.ts (Core Hook)...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$CORE_DIR/useAgentic.ts\\\" << 'USEAGENTIC'\\n/**\\n * useAgentic - THE core hook for all agentic features\\n * \\n * Provides:\\n * - Speech recognition (listening)\\n * - Text-to-speech (speaking)\\n * - Form field extraction\\n * - Command processing\\n * - Backend integration\\n */\\n\\nimport { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\\n\\ninterface AgenticConfig {\\n  context?: string;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n  onTranscript?: (text: string, isFinal: boolean) => void;\\n  onCommand?: (command: string, intent: string) => void;\\n  onFormData?: (fields: Record<string, string>) => void;\\n  onStateChange?: (state: AgenticState) => void;\\n}\\n\\ntype AgenticState = 'idle' | 'listening' | 'processing' | 'speaking' | 'error';\\n\\ninterface AgenticReturn {\\n  state: AgenticState;\\n  transcript: string;\\n  interimTranscript: string;\\n  isListening: boolean;\\n  isSpeaking: boolean;\\n  isProcessing: boolean;\\n  start: () => void;\\n  stop: () => void;\\n  toggle: () => void;\\n  speak: (text: string) => Promise<void>;\\n  processText: (text: string) => Promise<any>;\\n  fillField: (selector: string, value: string, animate?: boolean) => Promise<void>;\\n}\\n\\n// Singleton recognition instance\\nlet globalRecognition: SpeechRecognition | null = null;\\nlet globalSynth: SpeechSynthesis | null = null;\\n\\nexport function useAgentic(config: AgenticConfig = {}): AgenticReturn {\\n  const {\\n    context = 'general',\\n    autoStart = false,\\n    onTranscript,\\n    onCommand,\\n    onFormData,\\n    onStateChange\\n  } = config;\\n\\n  const [state, setState] = useState<AgenticState>('idle');\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [interimTranscript, setInterimTranscript] = useState('');\\n  \\n  const shouldRunRef = useRef(false);\\n  const isSpeakingRef = useRef(false);\\n  const contextRef = useRef(context);\\n  \\n  // Update context ref\\n  useEffect(() => { contextRef.current = context; }, [context]);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech services\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;\\n    \\n    globalSynth = window.speechSynthesis;\\n    \\n    if (!globalRecognition) {\\n      const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n      if (SR) {\\n        globalRecognition = new SR();\\n        globalRecognition.continuous = true;\\n        globalRecognition.interimResults = true;\\n        globalRecognition.lang = 'en-US';\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (autoStart) {\\n      setTimeout(() => start(), 500);\\n    }\\n    \\n    return () => {\\n      shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n    };\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Setup recognition handlers\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!globalRecognition) return;\\n\\n    const handleStart = () => {\\n      updateState('listening');\\n    };\\n\\n    const handleResult = async (event: SpeechRecognitionEvent) => {\\n      let interim = '';\\n      let final = '';\\n\\n      for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\\n        const text = event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n        if (event.results[i].isFinal) final += text;\\n        else interim += text;\\n      }\\n\\n      setInterimTranscript(interim);\\n      onTranscript?.(interim, false);\\n\\n      if (final.trim()) {\\n        setTranscript(final.trim());\\n        setInterimTranscript('');\\n        onTranscript?.(final.trim(), true);\\n        await processText(final.trim());\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    const handleError = (event: SpeechRecognitionErrorEvent) => {\\n      if (event.error === 'aborted' || event.error === 'no-speech') return;\\n      console.error('[useAgentic] Recognition error:', event.error);\\n      updateState('error');\\n    };\\n\\n    const handleEnd = () => {\\n      if (shouldRunRef.current && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\\n        setTimeout(() => {\\n          if (shouldRunRef.current && !isSpeakingRef.current) {\\n            safeStart();\\n          }\\n        }, 300);\\n      } else {\\n        updateState('idle');\\n      }\\n    };\\n\\n    globalRecognition.onstart = handleStart;\\n    globalRecognition.onresult = handleResult;\\n    globalRecognition.onerror = handleError;\\n    globalRecognition.onend = handleEnd;\\n  }, [onTranscript]);\\n\\n  const updateState = useCallback((newState: AgenticState) => {\\n    setState(newState);\\n    onStateChange?.(newState);\\n  }, [onStateChange]);\\n\\n  const safeStart = useCallback(() => {\\n    if (!globalRecognition) return;\\n    try {\\n      globalRecognition.start();\\n    } catch (e) {\\n      // Already started\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  const start = useCallback(() => {\\n    globalSynth?.cancel();\\n    isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n    shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n    updateState('listening');\\n    safeStart();\\n  }, [safeStart, updateState]);\\n\\n  const stop = useCallback(() => {\\n    shouldRunRef.current = false;\\n    try {\\n      globalRecognition?.stop();\\n    } catch {}\\n    globalSynth?.cancel();\\n    updateState('idle');\\n  }, [updateState]);\\n\\n  const toggle = useCallback(() => {\\n    if (shouldRunRef.current) stop();\\n    else start();\\n  }, [start, stop]);\\n\\n  const speak = useCallback(async (text: string): Promise<void> => {\\n    if (!globalSynth || !text) return;\\n    \\n    return new Promise((resolve) => {\\n      const wasRunning = shouldRunRef.current;\\n      isSpeakingRef.current = true;\\n      \\n      // Stop listening while speaking\\n      if (shouldRunRef.current) {\\n        try { globalRecognition?.stop(); } catch {}\\n      }\\n      \\n      globalSynth!.cancel();\\n      updateState('speaking');\\n      \\n      const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);\\n      utterance.rate = 0.95;\\n      utterance.pitch = 1;\\n      \\n      utterance.onend = () => {\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n        updateState('idle');\\n        \\n        if (wasRunning) {\\n          shouldRunRef.current = true;\\n          setTimeout(() => safeStart(), 300);\\n        }\\n        resolve();\\n      };\\n      \\n      utterance.onerror = () => {\\n        isSpeakingRef.current = false;\\n        updateState('idle');\\n        resolve();\\n      };\\n      \\n      globalSynth!.speak(utterance);\\n    });\\n  }, [safeStart, updateState]);\\n\\n  const processText = useCallback(async (text: string): Promise<any> => {\\n    updateState('processing');\\n    \\n    try {\\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/voice/command', {\\n        method: 'POST',\\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n        body: JSON.stringify({\\n          text,\\n          context: contextRef.current,\\n          user_type: 'user'\\n        })\\n      });\\n      \\n      const data = await response.json();\\n      \\n      // Handle intent/command\\n      if (data.analysis?.intent) {\\n        onCommand?.(text, data.analysis.intent);\\n      }\\n      \\n      // Handle form data\\n      if (data.formData?.fields && Object.keys(data.formData.fields).length > 0) {\\n        onFormData?.(data.formData.fields);\\n      }\\n      \\n      // Speak response\\n      if (data.response?.text && data.response?.speak !== false) {\\n        await speak(data.response.text);\\n      } else {\\n        updateState(shouldRunRef.current ? 'listening' : 'idle');\\n      }\\n      \\n      return data;\\n    } catch (err) {\\n      console.error('[useAgentic] Process error:', err);\\n      updateState(shouldRunRef.current ? 'listening' : 'idle');\\n      return null;\\n    }\\n  }, [onCommand, onFormData, speak, updateState]);\\n\\n  const fillField = useCallback(async (\\n    selector: string, \\n    value: string, \\n    animate: boolean = true\\n  ): Promise<void> => {\\n    const element = document.querySelector(selector) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\\n    if (!element) {\\n      console.warn('[useAgentic] Element not found:', selector);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    element.focus();\\n    element.classList.add('agentic-filling');\\n    \\n    if (animate) {\\n      // Typewriter effect\\n      element.value = '';\\n      for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\\n        element.value = value.substring(0, i);\\n        element.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));\\n        element.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));\\n        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 25));\\n      }\\n    } else {\\n      element.value = value;\\n      element.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));\\n      element.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));\\n    }\\n    \\n    element.classList.remove('agentic-filling');\\n    element.classList.add('agentic-filled');\\n    setTimeout(() => element.classList.remove('agentic-filled'), 1000);\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  return {\\n    state,\\n    transcript,\\n    interimTranscript,\\n    isListening: state === 'listening',\\n    isSpeaking: state === 'speaking',\\n    isProcessing: state === 'processing',\\n    start,\\n    stop,\\n    toggle,\\n    speak,\\n    processText,\\n    fillField\\n  };\\n}\\n\\nexport default useAgentic;\\nUSEAGENTIC\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 useAgentic.ts\\\"\\n\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\n# 2. UnifiedAgenticBar.tsx - THE ONE BAR\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83c\\udf9b\\ufe0f Creating UnifiedAgenticBar.tsx...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$CORE_DIR/UnifiedAgenticBar.tsx\\\" << 'UNIFIEDBAR'\\n/**\\n * UnifiedAgenticBar - THE ONE AGENTIC BAR Text-to-speech\\n * - Form filling\\n * - Waveform animation\\n * - Customizable appearance\\n */\\n\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';\\nimport { useAgentic } from './useAgentic';\\n\\ninterface FieldMapping {\\n  [voiceKey: string]: string | { selector: string; setter?: (value: string) => void };\\n}\\n\\ninterface UnifiedAgenticBarProps {\\n  // Behavior\\n  context?: string;\\n  fields?: FieldMapping;\\n  autoStart?: boolean;\\n  \\n  // Callbacks\\n  onCommand?: (command: string, intent: string) => void;\\n  onTranscript?: (text: string) => void;\\n  onFill?: (field: string, value: string) => void;\\n  speak?: (text: string) => void;\\n  \\n  // Appearance\\n  position?: 'fixed' | 'inline' | 'bottom' | 'top';\\n  variant?: 'full' | 'minimal' | 'rgba(0,0,0,0.1)', accent: '#0891b2' },\\n  teal: { bg: 'rgba(0, 66, 54, 0.95)', border: 'rgba(184, 134, 11, 0.4)', accent: '#B8860B' },\\n  gold: { bg: 'rgba(30, 30, 30, 0.95)', border: 'rgba(184, 134, 11, 0.5)', accent: '#B8860B' }\\n};\\n\\nexport const UnifiedAgenticBar: React.FC<UnifiedAgenticBarProps> = ({\\n  context = 'general',\\n  fields = {},\\n  autoStart = false,\\n  onCommand,\\n  onTranscript,\\n  onFill,\\n  speak: externalSpeak,\\n  position = 'inline',\\n  variant = 'full',\\n  theme = 'teal',\\n  hints = 'Speak naturally or type below...',\\n  showInput = true,\\n              {agentic.isSpeaking && '\\ud83d\\udd0a SPEAKING'}\\n              {agentic.isProcessing && '\\u26a1 PROCESSING'}\\n              {agentic.state === 'idle' && '\\ud83c\\udf99\\ufe0f </div>\\n          <span style={{\\n            fontSize: 10, padding: '3px 10px', borderRadius: 10,\\n            background: `${colors.accent}30`, color: colors.accent\\n          }}>\\n            INTERACTIVE\\n          </span>\\n        </div>\\n        \\n        {/* Waveform */}\\n        {agentic.isListening && (\\n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 3,  <span style={{ color: '#06b6d4', fontSize: 13 }}>\\u26a1 Filling {filling}...</span>\\n          </div>\\n        )}\\n        \\n        {/* Transcript */}\\n        <div style={{\\n          <div>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#10b981', fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600 }}>\\u2713 HEARD</span>\\n              <p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', margin: '6px 0 0', fontSize: 14 walkSpeed, onVisit, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // Start walking\\n  const startWalking = useCallback(() => {\\n    const found = discoverElements();\\n    if (found.length === 0) return;\\n    \\n    walkingRef.current = true;\\n    setIsWalking(true);\\n    setIsVisible(true);\\n    setCurrentIndex(0);\\n    \\n    // Move to first element\\n    moveToElement(found[0]);\\n    onVisit?.(found[0], 0);\\n    \\n    timeoutRef.current = setTimeout(walkNext, walkSpeed);\\n  }, [discoverElements, moveToElement, walkNext, walkSpeed, onVisit]);\\n\\n  // Stop walking\\n  const stopWalking = timeoutRef.current = null;\\n    }\\n  }, []);\\n\\n  // Toggle walking\\n  const toggleWalking = useCallback(() => {\\n    if (isWalking) stopWalking();\\n    else startWalking();\\n  }, [isWalking, startWalking, stopWalking]);\\n\\n  // Auto-start\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (enabled && autoStart) {\\n      const timer = setTimeout(startWalking, 1000);\\n      return () => }, []);\\n\\n  // Re-discover on resize\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const handleResize = () => discoverElements();\\n    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);\\n    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);\\n  }, [discoverElements]);\\n\\n  if (!enabled || !isVisible) return null;\\n\\n  // Cursor variants\\n  const cursorStyles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {\\n    pointer: {\\n      width: 0, height: 0,\\n      borderLeft: `${size/2}px solid transparent`,\\n      borderRight: `${size/2}px solid transparent`,\\n      borderBottom: `${size}px solid ${color}`,\\n      transform: 'rotate(-45deg)'\\n    },\\n    dot: {\\n      width: size, height: size,\\n      borderRadius: '50%',\\n      background: color,\\n      boxShadow: `0 0 ${size}px ${color}`\\n    },\\n    glow: {\\n      width: size * 2, height: size * 2,\\n      borderRadius: '50%',\\n      background: `radial-gradient(circle, ${color} 0%, transparent 70%)`,\\n      opacity: 0.8\\n    },\\n    hand: {\\n      fontSize: size,\\n      lineHeight: 1\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  return (\\n    <>\\n      <div\\n        style={{\\n          position: 'absolute',\\n          left: position.x,\\n          top: position.y,\\n          transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',\\n          pointerEvents: 'none',\\n          zIndex,\\n          transition: `all ${walkSpeed * 0.3}ms   onClick={toggleWalking}\\n        style={{\\n          position: 'fixed',\\n          bottom: 100,\\n          right: 20,\\n          width: 50,\\n          height: 50,\\n          borderRadius: | null = null;\\n      let fieldConfig: FieldConfig | null = null;\\n      \\n      for (const [name, config] of Object.entries(fields)) {\\n        const keys = config.voiceKeys || [name];\\n !fieldConfig) continue;\\n      \\n      const transformedValue = fieldConfig.transform ? fieldConfig.transform(value) : value;\\n      \\n      await agentic.fillField(fieldConfig.selector, filledFieldsRef.current.push(fieldName);\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    // Check if all fields filled\\n    if (filledFieldsRef.current.length === Object.keys(fields).length) {\\n \"\"\necho \"\ud83d\udce4 Creating UniversalUploader.tsx...\"\n\ncat > \"$CORE_DIR/UniversalUploader.tsx\" << 'UNIVERSALUPLOADER'\n/**\n * UniversalUploader - Handles ALL file formats\n * \n * data?: any;\n  error?: string;\n  preview?: string;\n}\n\ninterface UniversalUploaderProps {\n  // File types\n  accept?: string[];  // ['pdf', 'csv', 'xlsx', 'jpg', 'png', 'docx', 'json', 'xml']\n \n  // Voice\n  enableVoice?: boolean;\n  voiceContext?: string;\n  speak?: (text: string) => void;\n  \n  // Appearance\n  variant?: 'dropzone' | 'button' | 'minimal';\n  theme?: 'dark' | 'light' | 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet', icon: '\ud83d\udcd7', color: '#16a34a' },\n  xls: { mime: 'application/vnd.ms-excel', icon: '\ud83d\udcd7', color: '#16a34a' },\n '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', color: '#8b5cf6' },\n  gif: { mime: 'image/gif', icon: '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', color: '#ec4899' },\n  webp: { mime: 'image/webp', icon: '\ud83d\uddbc\ufe0f', color: '#06b6d4' },\n  docx: { mime: 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document', icon: '\ud83d\udcdd', color: '#2563eb' },\n  doc: { mime: 'application/msword', icon: '\ud83d\udcdd', color: '#2563eb' },\n  json: { mime: 'application/json', icon: '\ud83d\udccb', color: '#f97316' },\n  xml: { mime: 'application/xml', icon: '\ud83d\udccb', color: '#a855f7' },\n  txt: { mime: 'text/plain', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', text: '#e2e8f0' },\n  light: { bg: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)', border: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.1)', text: '#1e293b' },\n  teal: { bg: 'rgba(0, 66, 54, 0.9)', border: 'rgba(184, 134, 11, onUpload,\n  onProgress,\n  onError,\n  enableVoice = true,\n  voiceContext = 'upload',\n  speak,\n  variant = 'dropzone',\n  theme = 'teal',\n  showPreview = true,\n  children,\n  className = '',\n  style = {}\n}) => {\n  const [files, setFiles] = useState<File[]>([]);\n  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);\n  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);\n  const [results, Build accept string\n  const acceptString = accept.map(ext => FILE_TYPES[ext]?.mime || `.${ext}`).join(',');\n  \n  // Voice control\n  const agentic = useAgentic({\n    context: voiceContext,\n    onCommand: (cmd, intent) => {\n      const lower = cmd.toLowerCase();\n      if (lower.includes('upload') || lower.includes('select') || lower.includes('file') || lower.includes('choose')) {\n        fileInputRef.current?.click();\n      }\n      if (lower.includes('clear') || lower.includes('remove')) {\n        clearFiles();\n      }\n    }\n  });\n  \n  const speakFn = speak || agentic.speak;\n  \n  // Validate file\n  const validateFile = (file: File): string | null => {\n    const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\n    if (!accept.includes(ext) && !accept.includes('*')) {\n      return `File type .${ext} not allowed`;\n    }\n    if (file.size > maxSize * 1024 * 1024) {\n      return `File too large (max ${maxSize}MB)`;\n    }\n    return null;\n  };\n  \n  // Handle files\n  const handleFiles = useCallback(async (fileList: FileList | File[]) => {\n    const newFiles = Array.from(fileList);\n    const validFiles: File[] = [];\n    \n    for (const file of newFiles) {\n      const error = validateFile(file);\n      if (error) {\n        onError?.(error);\n        speakFn?.(`Cannot upload ${file.name}. ${error}`);\n      } else {\n        validFiles.push(file);\n      }\n    }\n    \n    if (validFiles.length === 0) return;\n    \n    setFiles(prev => multiple ? [...prev, ...validFiles] : validFiles);\n    speakFn?.(`Selected ${validFiles.length} file${validFiles.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`);\n    \n    // Auto-upload\n    await uploadFiles(validFiles);\n  }, [accept, maxSize, multiple, onError, speakFn]);\n  \n  // Upload files to backend\n  const uploadFiles = async (filesToUpload: File[]) => {\n    setUploading(true);\n    setProgress(0);\n    \n    const uploadResults: FileResult[] = [];\n    const totalFiles = filesToUpload.length;\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i < totalFiles; i++) {\n      const file = filesToUpload[i];\n      const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\n      \n      try {\n        const formData = new FormData();\n        formData.append('file', file);\n        formData.append('fileType', ext);\n        \n        // Determine endpoint based on file type\n        let endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/file';\n        if (['pdf'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/pdf';\n        else if (['csv', 'xlsx', 'xls'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/spreadsheet';\n        else if (['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'webp'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/image';\n        else if (['docx', 'doc'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/document';\n        \n        const response = await fetch(endpoint, {\n          method: 'POST',\n          body: formData\n        });\n        \n        const data = await response.json();\n        \n        uploadResults.push({\n          file,\n          success: response.ok && (data.success !== false),\n          data,\n          preview: ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'webp'].includes(ext) \n            ? err.message || 'Upload failed'\n        });\n      }\n      \n      const newProgress = Math.round(((i + 1) / totalFiles) * 100);\n      setProgress(newProgress);\n      onProgress?.(newProgress);\n    }\n    \n    setResults(uploadResults);\n    setUploading(false);\n    onUpload?.(uploadResults);\n    \n    const successCount = uploadResults.filter(r => r.success).length;\n    speakFn?.(`Uploaded ${successCount} of ${totalFiles} files successfully`);\n  };\n  \n  // Clear files\n  const clearFiles = () => {\n    setFiles([]);\n    setResults([]);\n    setProgress(0);\n  };\n  \n  // Drag handlers\n  const handleDrag = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    e.stopPropagation();\n  };\n  \n  const handleDragIn = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    e.stopPropagation();\n    setDragActive(true);\n  };\n  \n  const handleDragOut = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    e.stopPropagation();\n    setDragActive(false);\n  };\n  \n  const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    e.stopPropagation();\n    setDragActive(false);\n    if (e.dataTransfer.files && e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {\n      handleFiles(e.dataTransfer.files);\n    }\n  };\n  \n  // Get file icon\n  const getFileIcon = (fileName: string) => {\n    const ext = fileName.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\n    return || '#64748b';\n  };\n  \n  if (variant === 'button') {\n    return (\n      <div className={className} style={style}>\n        <input\n          ref={fileInputRef}\n          type=\"file\"\n          accept={acceptString}\n          multiple={multiple}\n          onChange={e => e.target.files && handleFiles(e.target.files)}\n          style={{ display: 'none' }}\n        />\n        <button\n '#06b6d4' : colors.border}`,\n          borderRadius: 16,\n          padding: 40,\n          textAlign: 'center',\n          cursor: uploading ? 'wait' : 'pointer',\n          background: dragActive ? 'rgba(6, 182, 212, 0.1)' : colors.bg,\n          transition: 'all 0.3s'\n        }}\n      >\n        {children || (\n          <>\n            {uploading ? (\n              <>\n                <div style={{ fontSize: 48, marginBottom: 16 }}>\ud83d\udce4</div>\n                <p style={{ color: colors.text, fontSize: 16, margin: '0 0 12px' }}>\n                  Uploading... {progress}%\n                </p>\n                <div style={{\n                  height: 8, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 4,\n                  overflow: 'hidden', maxWidth: 300, margin: '0 auto'\n                }}>\n                  <div style={{\n                    width: `${progress}%`, height: '100%',\n                    background: 'linear-gradient(90deg, #06b6d4, #8b5cf6)',\n                    transition: 'width 0.3s'\n                  }} />\n                </div>\n              </>\n            ) : (\n              <>\n                <div style={{ fontSize: 48, marginBottom: 16 }}>\n                  {dragActive ? '\ud83d\udce5' : '\ud83d\udcc1'}\n                </div>\n                <p style={{ color: colors.text, fontSize: 16, margin: '0 0 8px' }}>\n                  {dragActive ? 's' : ''} uploaded\n            </span>\n            <button\n              onClick={clearFiles}\n              style={{\n                background: 'transparent', border: 'none',\n                color: '#ef4444', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 13\n              }}\n            >\n              Clear all\n            </button>\n          </div>\n          \n          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>\n            {results.map((result, i) => (\n              <div\n                key={i}\n                style={{\n                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,\n                  padding: '10px 14px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',\n                  borderRadius: 10, border: `1px solid ${result.success ? },\\n  xls: { mime: 'application/vnd.ms-excel', icon: '\\ud83d\\udcd7', color: '#16a34a' },\\n  jpg: { mime: 'image/jpeg', icon: '\\ud83d\\uddbc\\ufe0f', color: '#f59e0b' },\\n  jpeg: { mime: },\\n  json: { mime: 'application/json', icon: '\\ud83d\\udccb', color: '#f97316' },\\n  xml: { mime: 'application/xml', icon: '\\ud83d\\udccb', color: '#a855f7' },\\n  txt: { mime: 'text/plain', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', text: '#e2e8f0' },\\n  light: { bg: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)', border: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.1)', text: '#1e293b' },\\n  teal: { bg: 'rgba(0, 66, 54, 0.9)', border: 'rgba(184, 134,  context: voiceContext,\\n    onCommand: (cmd, intent) => {\\n      const lower = cmd.toLowerCase();\\n      if (lower.includes('upload') || lower.includes('select') || lower.includes('file') || lower.includes('choose')) {\\n        fileInputRef.current?.click();\\n      }\\n      if (lower.includes('clear') || lower.includes('remove')) {\\n        clearFiles();\\n      }\\n    }\\n  });\\n  \\n  const speakFn = speak || agentic.speak;\\n  \\n  // Validate file\\n  const validateFile = (file: File): string | null => {\\n    const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\\n ${maxSize}MB)`;\\n    }\\n    return null;\\n  };\\n  \\n  // Handle files\\n  const handleFiles = useCallback(async (fileList: FileList | File[]) => {\\n    const newFiles = Array.from(fileList);\\n    const validFiles: File[] = [];\\n    \\n    for (const file of newFiles) {\\n      const error = validateFile(file);\\n      if (error) {\\n        onError?.(error);\\n        speakFn?.(`Cannot upload ${file.name}. ${error}`);\\n      } else {\\n        validFiles.push(file);\\n      }\\n    }\\n    \\n    if (validFiles.length === 0) return;\\n    \\n    setFiles(prev => multiple ? [...prev, ...validFiles] : validFiles);\\n    speakFn?.(`Selected ${validFiles.length} file${validFiles.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`);\\n    \\n    // Auto-upload\\n    await uploadFiles(validFiles);\\n  }, [accept, maxSize, multiple, onError, speakFn]);\\n  \\n  // Upload files to backend\\n  const uploadFiles = async (filesToUpload: File[]) => {\\n    setUploading(true);\\n    setProgress(0);\\n    \\n    const uploadResults: FileResult[] = [];\\n    const totalFiles = filesToUpload.length;\\n    \\n    for (let i = 0; i < totalFiles; i++) {\\n      const file = filesToUpload[i];\\n      const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\\n      \\n      try {\\n        const formData = new FormData();\\n        formData.append('file', file);\\n        formData.append('fileType', ext);\\n        \\n        // Determine endpoint based on file type\\n        let endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/file';\\n        if (['pdf'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/pdf';\\n        else if (['csv', 'xlsx', 'xls'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/spreadsheet';\\n        else if (['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'webp'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/image';\\n        else if (['docx', 'doc'].includes(ext)) endpoint = 'http://localhost:1117/api/upload/document';\\n        \\n        const response = await fetch(endpoint, {\\n          method: 'POST',\\n          body: formData\\n        });\\n        \\n        const data = await response.json();\\n        \\n        uploadResults.push({\\n          file,\\n          success: response.ok && (data.success !== false),\\n          data,\\n          preview: ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'webp'].includes(ext) \\n            ? URL.createObjectURL(file) \\n            : undefined\\n        });\\n        \\n      } catch (err: any) {\\n        uploadResults.push({\\n          file,\\n          success: false,\\n          error: err.message || 'Upload failed'\\n        });\\n      }\\n      \\n      const newProgress = Math.round(((i + 1) / totalFiles) * 100);\\n      setProgress(newProgress);\\n      onProgress?.(newProgress);\\n    }\\n    \\n    setResults(uploadResults);\\n    setUploading(false);\\n    onUpload?.(uploadResults);\\n    \\n    const successCount = uploadResults.filter(r => r.success).length;\\n    speakFn?.(`Uploaded ${successCount} of ${totalFiles} files successfully`);\\n  };\\n  \\n  // Clear files\\n  const clearFiles = () => {\\n    setFiles([]);\\n    setResults([]);\\n    setProgress(0);\\n  };\\n  \\n  // Drag handlers\\n  const handleDrag = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\\n    e.preventDefault();\\n    e.stopPropagation();\\n  };\\n  \\n  const handleDragIn = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\\n    e.preventDefault();\\n    e.stopPropagation();\\n    setDragActive(true);\\n  };\\n  \\n  const handleDragOut = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\\n    e.preventDefault();\\n    e.stopPropagation();\\n    setDragActive(false);\\n  };\\n  \\n  const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\\n    e.preventDefault();\\n    e.stopPropagation();\\n    setDragActive(false);\\n    if (e.dataTransfer.files && e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {\\n      handleFiles(e.dataTransfer.files);\\n    }\\n  };\\n  \\n  // Get file icon\\n  const getFileIcon = (fileName: string) => {\\n    const ext = fileName.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() || '';\\n    return FILE_TYPES[ext]?.icon || '\\ud83d\\udcc4';\\n  };\\n  \\n  const getFileColor = (fileName: <div>\\n              <h2 style={{ color: '#fff', margin: 0, fontSize: '1.1em' }}>{title}</h2>\\n              <span style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.8em' }}>\\n                Step {steps.map((step, i) => (\\n            <div\\n              key={step.id}\\n              onClick={() => i < currentStepIndex && goToStep(i)}\\n              style={{\\n                flex: 1,\\n                height: 4,\\n                borderRadius: 2,\\n                background: i <= currentStepIndex ? theme.accent : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)',\\n                cursor: i < currentStepIndex updateData,\\n  onNext,\\n  speak,\\n  isActive\\n}) => {\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState(data.phone || '');\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (isActive) {\\n      speak(\\\"Please enter your (value: string) => {\\n    const formatted = formatPhone(value);\\n    setPhone(formatted);\\n    updateData({ phone: formatted.replace(/-/g, '') });\\n  };\\n\\n  const isValid = phone.replace(/-/g, '').length === 10;\\n\\n  const handleSubmit = () => {\\n    if (isValid) {\\n      speak(\\\"Sending verification code.\\\");\\n      onNext();\\n    } else {\\n      speak(\\\"Please enter a valid <span style={{ fontSize: '3em' }}>\\ud83d\\udd10</span>\\n      <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: 0 }}>Enter Verification Code</h3>\\n      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em', (!isActive) return;\\n    \\n    const steps = [\\n      { p: 20, s: 'Processing uploads...' },\\n      { p: 40, s: 'Extracting data...' },\\n      { p: 60, s: 'Analyzing content...' },\\n      { p: 'flow' : 'selector');\n  const [selectedFlow, setSelectedFlow] = useState<FlowType>(initialFlow);\n\n  const handleSelectFlow = (flowType: FlowType) => {\n    setSelectedFlow(flowType);\n    setState('flow');\n  };\n\n  const handleBack = () => {\n    setSelectedFlow(null);\n    setState('selector');\n  };\n\n  const handleFlowComplete = (data: Record<string, any>) => {\n analyzeIntent(text) {\n    const lower = (text || '').toLowerCase();\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who|how many/)) return 'query';\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit/)) return 'control';\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|upload/)) return 'action';\n    if (lower.match(/company|business|name|agency/)) return 'form_input';\n    if (lower.match(/phone|number|digit/)) return 'phone_input';\n    if (lower.match(/beautify|enhance|improve/)) return 'beautify';\n    return 'general';\n}\n\nfunction extractFormData(text, context) {\n    const result = { fields: {} };\n    \n    // Company name\n    let match = text.match(/company\\s+(?:is|name\\s+is|called)\\s+[\"']?([^\"'\\.,]+)/i);\n    if (match) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\n    \n    match = text.match(/(?:i am from|this is|we are|my name is)\\s+[\"']?([^\"'\\.,]+?)(?:\\s+and|\\s*$)/i);\n    if (match && !result.fields.companyName) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\n    \n    // Description\n    match = text.match(/(?:we\\s+)?(?:sell|manufacture|make|produce|provide|offer|build|construct)\\s+(.+)/i);\n    if (match) result.fields.description = match[1].trim();\n    \n    // Phone - convert words to digits\n    const numberWords = { zero:'0', one:'1', two:'2', three:'3', four:'4', five:'5', six:'6', seven:'7', eight:'8', nine:'9', oh:'0' };\n    let phoneText = (text || '').toLowerCase();\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\n        phoneText = phoneText.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\b${word}\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\n    }\n    const digits = phoneText.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    if (digits.length >= 10) result.fields.phone = digits.slice(0, 10);\n    if (context === 'otp' && digits.length === 6) result.fields.otp = digits;\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\nasync \\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\\n    const lower = (text || '').toLowerCase();\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who|how many/)) return 'query';\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit/)) return 'control';\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|upload/)) return 'action';\\n    if (lower.match(/company|business|name|agency/)) return 'form_input';\\n    if (lower.match(/phone|number|digit/)) return 'phone_input';\\n    if (lower.match(/beautify|enhance|improve/)) return 'beautify';\\n    return 'general';\\n}\\n\\nfunction extractFormData(text, context) {\\n    const result = { fields: {} };\\n    \\n    // Company name\\n    let match = text.match(/company\\\\s+(?:is|name\\\\s+is|called)\\\\s+[\\\"']?([^\\\"'\\\\.,]+)/i);\\n    if (match) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\\n    \\n    match = text.match(/(?:i am from|this is|we are|my name is)\\\\s+[\\\"']?([^\\\"'\\\\.,]+?)(?:\\\\s+and|\\\\s*$)/i);\\n    if (match && !result.fields.companyName) result.fields.companyName = match[1].trim();\\n    \\n    // Description\\n    match = text.match(/(?:we\\\\s+)?(?:sell|manufacture|make|produce|provide|offer|build|construct)\\\\s+(.+)/i);\\n    if (match) result.fields.description = match[1].trim();\\n    \\n    // Phone - convert words to digits\\n    const numberWords = { zero:'0', one:'1', two:'2', three:'3', four:'4', five:'5', six:'6', seven:'7', eight:'8', nine:'9', oh:'0' };\\n    let phoneText = (text || '').toLowerCase();\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) {\\n        phoneText = phoneText.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\\\\\b${word}\\\\\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\\n    }\\n    const digits = phoneText.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    if (digits.length >= 10) result.fields.phone = digits.slice(0, 10);\\n    if (context === 'otp' && digits.length === 6) result.fields.otp = digits;\\n    \\n    return result;\\n}\\n\\nasync function getAllTableCounts() {\\n    const counts = {};\\n    try {\\n        const tables = (await pool.query(\\\"SELECT tablename FROM pg_tables WHERE schemaname='public'\\\")).rows;\\n        for (const { tablename } of tables) {\\n            try { counts[tablename] = parseInt((await pool.query(`SELECT COUNT(*) FROM
